namespace = ab_diocese_project
normal_or_historical_nations = yes

#Tsarevets - Tier 2
country_event = {
	id = ab_diocese_project.1
	title = ab_diocese_project.1.t
	desc = ab_diocese_project.1.d
	picture = BAD_WITH_MONARCH_eventPicture
	
	hidden = yes
	
	trigger = {
		tag = ROM
		has_government_attribute = ab_diocese_projects
		NOT = { has_country_modifier = diocese_project_tsarevets2 }
		4704 = {
			owner = {
				is_subject_of = ROM
				is_subject_of_type = diocese_vassal
			}
			has_great_project = {
				type = tsarevets
				tier = 2
			}
			NOT = {
				has_great_project = {
					type = tsarevets
					tier = 3
				}
			}
			culture_group = roman_g
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = ab_diocese_project.1.a
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = diocese_project_tsarevets2
			duration = -1
			hidden = yes
		}
	}
}

#Tsarevets - Tier 3
country_event = {
	id = ab_diocese_project.2
	title = ab_diocese_project.2.t
	desc = ab_diocese_project.2.d
	picture = BAD_WITH_MONARCH_eventPicture
	
	hidden = yes
	
	trigger = {
		tag = ROM
		has_government_attribute = ab_diocese_projects
		NOT = { has_country_modifier = diocese_project_tsarevets3 }
		4704 = {
			owner = {
				is_subject_of = ROM
				is_subject_of_type = diocese_vassal
			}
			has_great_project = {
				type = tsarevets
				tier = 3
			}
			culture_group = roman_g
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = ab_diocese_project.2.a
		remove_country_modifier = diocese_project_tsarevets2
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = diocese_project_tsarevets3
			duration = -1
			hidden = yes
		}
	}
}

#Tsarevets - Remove
country_event = {
	id = ab_diocese_project.3
	title = ab_diocese_project.3.t
	desc = ab_diocese_project.3.d
	picture = BAD_WITH_MONARCH_eventPicture
	
	hidden = yes
	
	trigger = {
		tag = ROM
		OR = {
			has_country_modifier = diocese_project_tsarevets2
			has_country_modifier = diocese_project_tsarevets3
		}
		OR = {
			NOT = {
				has_government_attribute = ab_diocese_projects
			}
			4704 = {
				OR = {
					owner = {
						NOT = {
							AND = {
								is_subject_of = ROM
								is_subject_of_type = diocese_vassal
							}
						}
					}
					NOT = { culture_group = roman_g }
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = ab_diocese_project.3.a
		remove_country_modifier = diocese_project_tsarevets2
		remove_country_modifier = diocese_project_tsarevets3
	}
}

#Rila Monasteries - Tier 1
country_event = {
	id = ab_diocese_project.4
	title = ab_diocese_project.4.t
	desc = ab_diocese_project.4.d
	picture = BAD_WITH_MONARCH_eventPicture
	
	hidden = yes
	
	trigger = {
		tag = ROM
		has_government_attribute = ab_diocese_projects
		NOT = { has_country_modifier = diocese_project_rila1 }
		4703 = {
			owner = {
				is_subject_of = ROM
				is_subject_of_type = diocese_vassal
				religion = orthodox
			}
			has_great_project = {
				type = rila_monasteries
				tier = 1
			}
			NOT = {
				has_great_project = {
					type = rila_monasteries
					tier = 2
				}
			}
			religion = orthodox
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = ab_diocese_project.4.a
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = diocese_project_rila1
			duration = -1
			hidden = yes
		}
	}
}

#Rila Monasteries - Remove
country_event = {
	id = ab_diocese_project.7
	title = ab_diocese_project.7.t
	desc = ab_diocese_project.7.d
	picture = BAD_WITH_MONARCH_eventPicture
	
	hidden = yes
	
	trigger = {
		tag = ROM
		OR = {
			has_country_modifier = diocese_project_rila1
			has_country_modifier = diocese_project_rila2
			has_country_modifier = diocese_project_rila3
		}
		OR = {
			NOT = {
				has_government_attribute = ab_diocese_projects
			}
			4703 = {
				owner = {
					NOT = {
						is_subject_of = ROM
						is_subject_of_type = diocese_vassal
						religion = orthodox
					}
				}
			}
			4703 = {
				NOT = { religion = orthodox }
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = ab_diocese_project.7.a
		remove_country_modifier = diocese_project_rila1
		remove_country_modifier = diocese_project_rila2
		remove_country_modifier = diocese_project_rila3
	}
}

	trigger = {
		tag = ROM

		116 = {
			owner = {
				is_subject_of = ROM
				is_subject_of_type = diocese_vassal
				religion_group = christian
			}
			has_great_project = {
				type = santa_maria_del_fiore
				tier = 1
			}
			NOT = {
				has_great_project = {
					type = santa_maria_del_fiore

				}
			}

	id = ab_diocese_project.140
	title = ab_diocese_project.140.t
	desc = ab_diocese_project.140.d
	picture = BAD_WITH_MONARCH_eventPicture
	
	hidden = yes
	
	trigger = {
		tag = ROM
		has_government_attribute = ab_diocese_projects
		NOT = { has_country_modifier = diocese_project_bergen3 }
		23 = {
			owner = {
				is_subject_of = ROM
				is_subject_of_type = diocese_vassal
			}
			has_great_project = {
				type = bergen
				tier = 3
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = ab_diocese_project.140.a
		remove_country_modifier = diocese_project_bergen1
		remove_country_modifier = diocese_project_bergen2
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = diocese_project_bergen3
			duration = -1
			hidden = yes
		}
	}
}

#Bergen Entrepot - Remove
country_event = {
	id = ab_diocese_project.141
	title = ab_diocese_project.141.t
	desc = ab_diocese_project.141.d
	picture = BAD_WITH_MONARCH_eventPicture
	
	hidden = yes
	
	trigger = {
		tag = ROM
		OR = {
			has_country_modifier = diocese_project_bergen1
			has_country_modifier = diocese_project_bergen2
			has_country_modifier = diocese_project_bergen3
		}
		OR = {
			NOT = {
				has_government_attribute = ab_diocese_projects
			}
			23 = {
				owner = {
					NOT = {
						is_subject_of = ROM
						is_subject_of_type = diocese_vassal
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = ab_diocese_project.141.a
		remove_country_modifier = diocese_project_bergen1
		remove_country_modifier = diocese_project_bergen2
		remove_country_modifier = diocese_project_bergen3
	}
}

#Bibliotheca Corviniana - Tier 1
country_event = {
	id = ab_diocese_project.142
	title = ab_diocese_project.142.t
	desc = ab_diocese_project.142.d
	picture = BAD_WITH_MONARCH_eventPicture
	
	hidden = yes
	
	trigger = {
		tag = ROM
		has_government_attribute = ab_diocese_projects
		NOT = { has_country_modifier = diocese_project_bibliotheca1 }
		153 = {
			owner = {
				is_subject_of = ROM
				is_subject_of_type = diocese_vassal
			}
			has_great_project = {
				type = buda_castle
				tier = 1
			}
			NOT = {
				has_great_project = {
					type = buda_castle
					tier = 2
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = ab_diocese_project.142.a
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = diocese_project_bibliotheca1
			duration = -1
			hidden = yes
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = ab_diocese_project.149
	title = ab_diocese_project.149.t
	desc = ab_diocese_project.149.d
	picture = BAD_WITH_MONARCH_eventPicture
	
	hidden = yes
	
	trigger = {
		tag = ROM
		OR = {
			has_country_modifier = diocese_project_brancastle1
			has_country_modifier = diocese_project_brancastle2
			has_country_modifier = diocese_project_brancastle3
		}
		OR = {
			NOT = {
				has_government_attribute = ab_diocese_projects
			}
			4128 = {
				OR = {
					owner = {
						NOT = {
							AND = {
								is_subject_of = ROM
								is_subject_of_type = diocese_vassal
							}
						}
					}
					NOT = { culture_group = roman_g }
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = ab_diocese_project.149.a
		remove_country_modifier = diocese_project_brancastle1
		remove_country_modifier = diocese_project_brancastle2
		remove_country_modifier = diocese_project_brancastle3
	}
}

#Jerusalem - Tier 1
country_event = {
	id = ab_diocese_project.158
	title = ab_diocese_project.158.t
	desc = ab_diocese_project.158.d
	picture = BAD_WITH_MONARCH_eventPicture
	
	hidden = yes
	
	trigger = {
		tag = ROM
		has_government_attribute = ab_diocese_projects
		NOT = { has_country_modifier = diocese_project_jerusalem1 }
		379 = {
			owner = {
				is_subject_of = ROM
				is_subject_of_type = diocese_vassal
			}
			has_great_project = {
				type = holy_city_jerusalem
				tier = 1
			}
			NOT = {
				has_great_project = {
					type = holy_city_jerusalem
					tier = 2
				}
			}
			OR = {
				religion_group = muslim
				religion_group = christian
			}
			has_owner_religion = yes
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = ab_diocese_project.158.a
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = diocese_project_jerusalem1
			duration = -1
			hidden = yes
		}
	}
}

	title = ab_diocese_project.320.t
	desc = ab_diocese_project.320.d
	picture = BAD_WITH_MONARCH_eventPicture
	
	hidden = yes
	
	trigger = {
		tag = ROM
		OR = {
			has_country_modifier = diocese_project_halicarnassus1
			has_country_modifier = diocese_project_halicarnassus2
			has_country_modifier = diocese_project_halicarnassus3
		}
		OR = {
			NOT = {
				has_government_attribute = ab_diocese_projects
			}
			319 = {
				owner = {
					NOT = {
						is_subject_of = ROM
						is_subject_of_type = diocese_vassal
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = ab_diocese_project.320.a
		remove_country_modifier = diocese_project_halicarnassus1
		remove_country_modifier = diocese_project_halicarnassus2
		remove_country_modifier = diocese_project_halicarnassus3
	}
}

#Nicene - Tier 2
country_event = {
	id = ab_diocese_project.321
	title = ab_diocese_project.321.t
	desc = ab_diocese_project.321.d
	picture = BAD_WITH_MONARCH_eventPicture
	
	hidden = yes
	
	trigger = {
		tag = ROM
		has_government_attribute = ab_diocese_projects
		NOT = { has_country_modifier = diocese_project_nicene2 }
		317 = {
			owner = {
				is_subject_of = ROM
				is_subject_of_type = diocese_vassal
				OR = {
					full_idea_group = offensive_ideas
					full_idea_group = quality_ideas
					full_idea_group = professional_ideas
				}
			}
			has_great_project = {
				type = nicene_academy
				tier = 2
			}
			NOT = {
				has_great_project = {
					type = nicene_academy
					tier = 3
				}
			}
		}
		OR = {
			full_idea_group = offensive_ideas
			full_idea_group = quality_ideas
			full_idea_group = professional_ideas
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = ab_diocese_project.321.a
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = diocese_project_nicene2
			duration = -1
			hidden = yes
		}
	}
}

				tier = 3
			}
		}
		OR = {
			full_idea_group = offensive_ideas
			full_idea_group = quality_ideas

#Nicene - Remove
country_event = {
	id = ab_diocese_project.323
	title = ab_diocese_project.323.t
	desc = ab_diocese_project.323.d
	picture = BAD_WITH_MONARCH_eventPicture
	
	hidden = yes
	
	trigger = {
		tag = ROM
		OR = {
			has_country_modifier = diocese_project_nicene2
			has_country_modifier = diocese_project_nicene3
		}
		OR = {
			NOT = {
				has_government_attribute = ab_diocese_projects
			}
			317 = {
				owner = {
					NOT = {
						AND = {
							is_subject_of = ROM
							is_subject_of_type = diocese_vassal
							OR = {
								full_idea_group = offensive_ideas
								full_idea_group = quality_ideas
								full_idea_group = professional_ideas
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			NOT = {
				OR = {
					full_idea_group = offensive_ideas
					full_idea_group = quality_ideas
					full_idea_group = professional_ideas
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = ab_diocese_project.323.a
		remove_country_modifier = diocese_project_nicene2
		remove_country_modifier = diocese_project_nicene3
	}
}

		tag = ROM

		NOT = { has_country_modifier = diocese_project_hagiasophia1 }
		151 = {
			owner = {
				is_subject_of = ROM
				is_subject_of_type = diocese_vassal
			}
			has_great_project = {
				type = hagia_sophia
				tier = 1
			}
			NOT = {
				has_great_project = {
					type = hagia_sophia
					tier = 2
				}
			}
			OR = {
				religion_group = muslim
				religion_group = christian
			}
			has_owner_religion = yes
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = ab_diocese_project.324.a
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = diocese_project_hagiasophia1
			duration = -1
			hidden = yes
		}
	}

				religion = catholic

				type = stpeters_cathedral

			}

			has_country_modifier = diocese_project_barakatra3
		}
		OR = {
			NOT = {
				has_government_attribute = ab_diocese_projects
			}
			564 = {
				owner = {
					NOT = {
						is_subject_of = ROM
						is_subject_of_type = diocese_vassal
						religion_group = muslim
					}
				}
			}
			564 = {
				NOT = { religion_group = muslim }
			}
			564 = {
				NOT = { culture_group = roman_g }
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = ab_diocese_project.383.a
		remove_country_modifier = diocese_project_barakatra1
		remove_country_modifier = diocese_project_barakatra2
		remove_country_modifier = diocese_project_barakatra3
